       </section>\r\n    </div>\r\n\r\n    <script>\r\n        // ===== ê³µí†µ ìœ í‹¸ =====\r\n        function setMetric(id, value) {\r\n            const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n            if (!el) return;\r\n\r\n            el.classList.remove(\"positive\", \"negative\");\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"m-symbol\" || id === \"m-price\" || id === \"m-equity\") {\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (id === \"maxdd\") {\r\n                el.style.color = \"#000000\";\r\n                if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                    el.style.color = \"#d00000\";\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = value;\r\n                return;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            if (typeof value === \"string\" && value.startsWith(\"-\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"negative\");\r\n            } else if (typeof value === \"string\" && value !== \"-\" && value !== \"0\" && !value.startsWith(\"0.\")) {\r\n                el.classList.add(\"positive\");\r\n            }\r\n            el.textContent = value;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatNumber(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return Number(v).toLocaleString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                minimumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n                maximumFractionDigits: digits,\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatPercent(v, digits = 2) {\r\n            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return \"-\";\r\n            return (Number(v) * 100).toFixed(digits) + \"%\";\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function formatTimeLabel(ts) {\r\n            try {\r\n                const d = new Date(ts);\r\n                if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n                return d.toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                    hour12: false,\r\n                    hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                });\r\n            } catch {\r\n                return String(ts ?? \"\");\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ ë²„í¼ =====\r\n        let maxPoints = 300;\r\n\r\n        const labelsHist = [];\r\n        const equityHist = [];\r\n        const priceHist = [];\r\n        const posHist = [];\r\n        const ddHist = [];\r\n        const ddWarnHist = [];\r\n        const ddCutHist = [];\r\n        const cumPnlHist = [];\r\n        const buyMarkersHist = [];\r\n        const sellMarkersHist = [];\r\n\r\n        // âœ… NEW: DD_WARN/DD_CUT \"ê¸°ì¤€ì„ \" ì‹œê³„ì—´(í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ë³€ê²½ ì‹œ êº¾ì„ì„ )\r\n        const ddWarnLineHist = [];\r\n        const ddCutLineHist = [];\r\n\r\n        // BUY / SELL ë§ˆì»¤ ê³„ì‚°ìš© ìƒíƒœ\r\n        let lastPos = null;\r\n\r\n        const BUY_MARK_Y = 0.4;\r\n        const SELL_MARK_Y = 0.6;\r\n\r\n        function trimHistoryArrays() {\r\n            const arrays = [\r\n                labelsHist,\r\n                equityHist,\r\n                priceHist,\r\n                posHist,\r\n                ddWarnHist,\r\n                ddCutHist,\r\n                ddHist,\r\n                cumPnlHist,\r\n                buyMarkersHist,\r\n                sellMarkersHist,\r\n\r\n                // âœ… NEW\r\n                ddWarnLineHist,\r\n                ddCutLineHist,\r\n            ];\r\n\r\n            arrays.forEach(arr => {\r\n                if (arr.length > maxPoints) {\r\n                    arr.splice(0, arr.length - maxPoints);\r\n                }\r\n            });\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function pushHistoryPoint(data) {\r\n            const nowTs = data.ts || data.time || new Date().toISOString();\r\n\r\n            const label = formatTimeLabel(nowTs);\r\n            const price = Number(data.price ?? data.px ?? 0);\r\n            const equity = Number(data.equity ?? data.eq ?? 0);\r\n            const pos = Number(data.position ?? data.pos ?? 0);\r\n            const ddRaw = Number(data.dd ?? data.drawdown ?? 0);\r\n            const cumPnl = Number(data.cum_pnl ?? data.cumpnl ?? data.pnl_cum ?? data.rpnl ?? 0);\r\n\r\n            let ddVal = ddRaw;\r\n            if (Math.abs(ddVal) > 1) ddVal = ddVal / 100.0;\r\n\r\n            labelsHist.push(label);\r\n            priceHist.push(price);\r\n            equityHist.push(equity);\r\n            posHist.push(pos);\r\n            ddHist.push(ddVal);\r\n\r\n            ddWarnHist.push(Number(data.dd_warn ?? 0));\r\n            ddCutHist.push(Number(data.dd_cut ?? 0));\r\n\r\n            cumPnlHist.push(cumPnl);\r\n\r\n            // ==== BUY/SELL ë§ˆì»¤: í¬ì§€ì…˜ ë³€í™” ê°ì§€ ====\r\n            let buyMark = null;\r\n            let sellMark = null;\r\n\r\n            const EPS = 0.00000001; // ê·¹ì†ŒëŸ‰ ë…¸ì´ì¦ˆëŠ” ë¬´ì‹œ\r\n\r\n            if (lastPos === null) {\r\n                lastPos = pos;\r\n            } else {\r\n                const diffPos = pos - lastPos;\r\n\r\n                if (Math.abs(diffPos) > EPS) {\r\n                    if (diffPos > 0) {\r\n                        buyMark = BUY_MARK_Y;\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        sellMark = SELL_MARK_Y;\r\n                    }\r\n                    lastPos = pos;\r\n                }\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            buyMarkersHist.push(buyMark);\r\n            sellMarkersHist.push(sellMark);\r\n\r\n            trimHistoryArrays();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°ì²´ =====\r\n        let mainChart = null;\r\n        let pnlChart = null;\r\n\r\n        // âœ… NEW: í˜„ì¬ ì„ íƒ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ì˜ DD_WARN/DD_CUT ê°’ ì½ê¸°(ë‹¨ì¼í™”)\r\n        function getActiveDdThresholds() {\r\n            const _rp = (window.riskProfilesByKey && window.uiActiveKey)\r\n                ? window.riskProfilesByKey[window.uiActiveKey]\r\n                : null;\r\n\r\n            const w = Number(_rp?.DD_WARN ?? window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_WARN ?? -0.002);\r\n            const c = Number(_rp?.DD_CUT ?? window.activeRiskProfile?.DD_CUT ?? -0.010);\r\n            return { ddWarnValue: w, ddCutValue: c };\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // âœ… NEW: DD ì¶•(yDD) ìë™ ë²”ìœ„(í˜„ì¬ DD + ê¸°ì¤€ì„  + ì•½ê°„ ì—¬ìœ )\r\n        function applyAutoDdAxis() {\r\n            if (!pnlChart) return;\r\n\r\n            // yDDëŠ” reverse:true ì´ë¯€ë¡œ\r\n            // í™”ë©´ ìœ„ìª½(ëœ ë§ˆì´ë„ˆìŠ¤/0 ê·¼ì²˜) = max\r\n            // í™”ë©´ ì•„ë˜ìª½(ë” ë§ˆì´ë„ˆìŠ¤) = min\r\n            const values = [];\r\n\r\n            // í˜„ì¬ DD íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬\r\n            for (const v of ddHist) {\r\n                const n = Number(v);\r\n                if (Number.isFinite(n)) values.push(n);\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // ê¸°ì¤€ì„  íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬(êº¾ì„ í¬í•¨)\r\n            for (const v of ddWarnLineHist) {\r\n                const n = Number(v);\r\n                if (Number.isFinite(n)) values.push(n);\r\n            }\r\n            for (const v of ddCutLineHist) {\r\n                const n = Number(v);\r\n                if (Number.isFinite(n)) values.push(n);\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // ê°’ì´ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ì¢…ë£Œ\r\n            if (values.length === 0) return;\r\n\r\n            let vmin = Math.min(...values); // ë” ë§ˆì´ë„ˆìŠ¤(ì•„ë˜)\r\n            let vmax = Math.max(...values); // 0ìª½(ìœ„)\r\n\r\n            // í•­ìƒ 0ì„ í¬í•¨(DDê°€ 0 ê·¼ì²˜ë¡œ ì˜¤ë©´ ì˜ë¦¼ ë°©ì§€)\r\n            vmax = Math.max(vmax, 0);\r\n\r\n            // ì—¬ìœ  í­(ë²”ìœ„ì˜ 15% ë˜ëŠ” ìµœì†Œ 0.002(0.2%p))\r\n            const span = Math.max(1e-9, vmax - vmin);\r\n            const pad = Math.max(span * 0.15, 0.002);\r\n\r\n            // reverse ì¶•ì—ì„œ ë³´ê¸° ì¢‹ê²Œ: ìœ„ìª½ì€ 0 ê·¼ì²˜, ì•„ë˜ìª½ì€ ë” ê¹Šê²Œ\r\n            const suggestedMax = Math.min(0, vmax + pad); // 0ì„ ë„˜ê¸°ì§€ ì•Šê²Œ\r\n            const suggestedMin = vmin - pad;\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.options.scales.yDD.suggestedMin = suggestedMin;\r\n            pnlChart.options.scales.yDD.suggestedMax = suggestedMax;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n\r\n        // âœ… NEW: í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ë³€ê²½ ìˆœê°„ì— \"êº¾ì„\"ì„ ê°•ì œë¡œ ë§Œë“¤ê¸° ìœ„í•œ 1í¬ì¸íŠ¸ ì£¼ì…\r\n        function injectThresholdKink() {\r\n            // íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ê°€ ì•„ì§ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´(ë¼ë²¨ì´ ì—†ìœ¼ë©´) ì£¼ì… ë¶ˆê°€\r\n            if (labelsHist.length === 0) return;\r\n\r\n            // í˜„ì¬ ì‹œê° ë¼ë²¨ í•˜ë‚˜ ì¶”ê°€ (ì¦‰ì‹œ êº¾ì„ í‘œì‹œìš©)\r\n            const label = formatTimeLabel(new Date().toISOString());\r\n            labelsHist.push(label);\r\n\r\n            // ë‹¤ë¥¸ ì‹œê³„ì—´ì€ \"ì§ì „ ê°’\"ì„ ë³µì œí•´ì„œ ê¸¸ì´ ë§ì¶¤(ì°¨íŠ¸ ê¹¨ì§ ë°©ì§€)\r\n            const last = (arr, fallback = null) => (arr.length ? arr[arr.length - 1] : fallback);\r\n\r\n            priceHist.push(last(priceHist, 0));\r\n            equityHist.push(last(equityHist, 0));\r\n            posHist.push(last(posHist, 0));\r\n            ddHist.push(last(ddHist, 0));\r\n            cumPnlHist.push(last(cumPnlHist, 0));\r\n\r\n            // ë§ˆì»¤ëŠ” ë¹ˆ ê°’(ì„  ì•ˆê·¸ë¦¼)\r\n            buyMarkersHist.push(null);\r\n            sellMarkersHist.push(null);\r\n\r\n            // âœ… í•µì‹¬: ê¸°ì¤€ì„ ì€ \"ìƒˆ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ê°’\"ìœ¼ë¡œ ì£¼ì… â†’ ì¦‰ì‹œ êº¾ì„ ìƒì„±\r\n            const { ddWarnValue, ddCutValue } = getActiveDdThresholds();\r\n            ddWarnLineHist.push(ddWarnValue);\r\n            ddCutLineHist.push(ddCutValue);\r\n\r\n            trimHistoryArrays();\r\n\r\n            // ì°¨íŠ¸ê°€ ìˆìœ¼ë©´ ì¦‰ì‹œ ë°˜ì˜\r\n            // (ë„¤ ì´ë¯¸ì§€ ê¸°ì¤€: 774~811í–‰ ê·¼ì²˜)\r\n            if (pnlChart) {\r\n                pnlChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n\r\n                pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...ddWarnLineHist];   // (ë„¤ ì´ë¯¸ì§€: 779í–‰ ìë¦¬)\r\n                pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...ddCutLineHist];    // (ë„¤ ì´ë¯¸ì§€: 780í–‰ ìë¦¬)\r\n\r\n                applyAutoDdAxis();   // âœ… ì—¬ê¸° 1ì¤„ ì¶”ê°€ (IIFE ëŒ€ì‹ )\r\n\r\n                pnlChart.update();   // (ë„¤ ì´ë¯¸ì§€: 809í–‰ ê·¼ì²˜)\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· + ì°¨íŠ¸ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateSnapshotAndCharts(data) {\r\n            const symbol = data.symbol ?? \"-\";\r\n            const price = data.price ?? null;\r\n            const pos = data.position ?? null;\r\n            const eq = data.equity ?? null;\r\n            const rpnl = data.rpnl ?? 0;\r\n            const upnl = data.upnl ?? 0;\r\n            const dd = data.dd ?? null;\r\n            const maxdd = data.max_dd ?? null;\r\n            const totalPnl = (rpnl || 0) + (upnl || 0);\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-symbol\", symbol);\r\n            setMetric(\"m-price\", formatNumber(price));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-position\", formatNumber(pos, 4));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-equity\", formatNumber(eq));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-pnl\", formatNumber(totalPnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-upnl\", formatNumber(upnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-rpnl\", formatNumber(rpnl));\r\n            setMetric(\"m-cumpnl\", formatNumber(data.cum_pnl ?? totalPnl));\r\n\r\n            setMetric(\"m-dd\", formatPercent(dd));\r\n            setMetric(\"maxdd\", formatPercent(maxdd));\r\n\r\n            const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n            if (lu) {\r\n                lu.textContent =\r\n                    \"Last update: \" +\r\n                    new Date().toLocaleTimeString(\"ko-KR\", {\r\n                        hour12: false,\r\n                        hour: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        minute: \"2-digit\",\r\n                        second: \"2-digit\",\r\n                    });\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // íˆìŠ¤í† ë¦¬ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ë°˜ì˜\r\n            pushHistoryPoint(data);\r\n\r\n            // âœ… NEW: ê¸°ì¤€ì„  ì‹œê³„ì—´ ëˆ„ì (í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ë³€ê²½ ì‹œ êº¾ì„ì„ )\r\n            const { ddWarnValue, ddCutValue } = getActiveDdThresholds();\r\n            ddWarnLineHist.push(ddWarnValue);\r\n            ddCutLineHist.push(ddCutValue);\r\n\r\n            trimHistoryArrays();\r\n\r\n            if (!mainChart || !pnlChart) return;\r\n\r\n            mainChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...equityHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...priceHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...cumPnlHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...buyMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.data.datasets[4].data = [...sellMarkersHist];\r\n            mainChart.update();\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.data.labels = [...labelsHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[0].data = [...posHist];\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[1].data = [...ddHist];\r\n\r\n            // âœ… NEW: â€œê¸°ì¤€ì„  êº¾ì„ì„ â€ì€ ëˆ„ì  ì‹œê³„ì—´ì„ ê·¸ëŒ€ë¡œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...ddWarnLineHist]; // label: \"DD_WARN\"\r\n            pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...ddCutLineHist];  // label: \"DD_CUT\"\r\n\r\n            pnlChart.update();\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ í—¬í¼ =====\r\n        async function fetchRiskProfileStatus() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const resp = await fetch(\"/api/risk-profile/active\");\r\n                if (!resp.ok) {\r\n                    console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì‹¤íŒ¨\", resp.status);\r\n                    return null;\r\n                }\r\n                return await resp.json();\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] fetch ì—ëŸ¬\", err);\r\n                return null;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ UI ë™ê¸°í™”(ì •ì„) =====\r\n        async function refreshRiskProfileUI() {\r\n            const data = await fetchRiskProfileStatus();\r\n            if (!data) return;\r\n\r\n            // âœ… DOMì€ í•¨ìˆ˜ ì•ˆì—ì„œ ë§¤ë²ˆ ì•ˆì „í•˜ê²Œ ì¡ëŠ”ë‹¤(ìŠ¤ì½”í”„ ë¬¸ì œ ì œê±°)\r\n            const select = document.getElementById(\"risk-profile-select\");\r\n            const label = document.getElementById(\"active-risk-profile\");\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ì—”ì§„ ê¸°ì¤€ ë‹¨ì¼í™”\r\n            const engineActive = data.engine_active_profile || \"neutral\";\r\n            const uiActive = engineActive;\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ì „ì—­ ìƒíƒœ(ë‹¨ì¼ ê¸°ì¤€)\r\n            window.riskProfilesByKey = data.profiles || {};\r\n            window.uiActiveKey = uiActive;\r\n            window.activeRiskProfile = window.riskProfilesByKey[uiActive] || null;\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ì½¤ë³´/ë¼ë²¨ ë™ê¸°í™”\r\n            if (select) select.value = engineActive;\r\n\r\n            if (label) {\r\n                const nameMap = { conservative: \"ë³´ìˆ˜í˜•\", neutral: \"ì¤‘ë¦½í˜•\", aggressive: \"ê³µê²©í˜•\" };\r\n                label.textContent = `í˜„ì¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼: ${nameMap[engineActive] || engineActive}`;\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // âœ… NEW: í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ë³€ê²½ ì¦‰ì‹œ â€œë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ê¸°ì¤€ì„  í¬ì¸íŠ¸â€ë¥¼ ìƒˆ ê°’ìœ¼ë¡œ ë³´ì •(ë°”ë¡œ í™”ë©´ ë°˜ì˜)\r\n            if (pnlChart && labelsHist.length > 0 && ddWarnLineHist.length > 0 && ddCutLineHist.length > 0) {\r\n                const { ddWarnValue, ddCutValue } = getActiveDdThresholds();\r\n                ddWarnLineHist[ddWarnLineHist.length - 1] = ddWarnValue;\r\n                ddCutLineHist[ddCutLineHist.length - 1] = ddCutValue;\r\n\r\n                pnlChart.data.datasets[2].data = [...ddWarnLineHist];\r\n                pnlChart.data.datasets[3].data = [...ddCutLineHist];\r\n\r\n                applyAutoDdAxis();\r\n\r\n                pnlChart.update();\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨ =====\r\n        async function refreshSnapshot() {\r\n            try {\r\n                const res = await fetch(\"/api/snapshot\");\r\n                if (!res.ok) throw new Error(\"snapshot http \" + res.status);\r\n\r\n                const data = await res.json();\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data\r\n\r\n                const banner = document.getElementById(\"alert-banner\");\r\n                const snap = document.querySelector(\"section.card.snapshot\");\r\n\r\n                if (!banner || !snap) return;   // âœ… ì—¬ê¸° ì¶”ê°€ (banner.className ì „ì—)\r\n\r\n                // âœ… cut-soon(âš ï¸ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ ê´€ë¦¬ ëŒ€ê¸° ì¤‘): FLAT(í¬ì§€ì…˜ 0)ì¼ ë•Œë§Œ í‘œì‹œ\r\n                const cutSoonEl = document.getElementById(\"cut-soon\");\r\n                if (cutSoonEl) {\r\n                    const pos = Number(data.position ?? 0);\r\n                    const shouldShow = Math.abs(pos) < 1e-12; // FLAT\r\n                    cutSoonEl.classList.toggle(\"hidden\", !shouldShow);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                banner.className = \"alert-banner hidden\";\r\n                snap.classList.remove(\"warn-border\", \"cut-border\");\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"WARN\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"âš  DD WARN\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"warn\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"warn-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                if (data.alert_level === \"CUT\") {\r\n                    banner.textContent = \"ğŸš¨ DD CUT\";\r\n                    banner.classList.remove(\"hidden\");\r\n                    banner.classList.add(\"cut\");\r\n                    snap.classList.add(\"cut-border\");\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                const level = (data.alert_level || \"OK\").toUpperCase();\r\n                const cls =\r\n                    level === \"CUT\" ? \"level-cut\" :\r\n                        level === \"WARN\" ? \"level-warn\" :\r\n                            \"level-ok\";\r\n\r\n                [\"m-dd\", \"m-dd-warn\", \"m-dd-cut\", \"m-alert-level\"].forEach(id => {\r\n                    const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                    if (!el) return;\r\n                    el.classList.remove(\"level-ok\", \"level-warn\", \"level-cut\");\r\n                    el.classList.add(cls);\r\n                });\r\n\r\n                // âœ… í•„ìš”í•˜ë©´ ë‹¤ë¥¸ ê³³ì—ì„œ ì¨ë„ ë˜ë„ë¡ ì „ì—­ì— ì €ì¥\r\n                window.snapshot_last = data;\r\n\r\n                // ğŸ”¢ DD / WARN / CUT / ALERT ê°’ ì„¸íŒ…\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-warn\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_warn * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-dd-cut\").innerText =\r\n                    (data.dd_cut * 100).toFixed(2) + \"%\";\r\n\r\n                document.getElementById(\"m-alert-level\").innerText =\r\n                    data.alert_level || \"-\";\r\n\r\n                // ìƒë‹¨ ì¹´ë“œ + ì°¨íŠ¸ ê°±ì‹ \r\n                updateSnapshotAndCharts(data);\r\n\r\n                // âœ… FLAT ìƒíƒœì¼ ë•Œë§Œ \"ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ ê´€ë¦¬ ëŒ€ê¸° ì¤‘\" í‘œì‹œ\r\n                if (cutSoonEl) {\r\n                    const pos = Number(data.position ?? 0);\r\n                    const shouldShow = Math.abs(pos) < 1e-12; // FLAT\r\n                    cutSoonEl.classList.toggle(\"hidden\", !shouldShow);\r\n                }\r\n\r\n                // âœ… ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ì€ ì „ì²´ ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·(data)ì„ ë„˜ê¸´ë‹¤\r\n                updateCostMetricsPanel(data);\r\n\r\n            } catch (err) {\r\n                console.error(\"snapshot error\", err);\r\n                const lu = document.getElementById(\"last-updated\");\r\n                if (lu) lu.textContent = \"ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ· ì˜¤ë¥˜\";\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== ë¹„ìš© íŒ¨ë„ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸ =====\r\n        function updateCostMetricsPanel(snapshot) {\r\n            if (!snapshot) return;\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ìŠ¤ëƒ…ìƒ·ì—ì„œ cost_metrics êº¼ë‚´ê¸°\r\n            const cm = snapshot.cost_metrics || {};\r\n\r\n            function put(id, value, digits = 2) {\r\n                const el = document.getElementById(id);\r\n                if (!el) return;\r\n                if (value === null || value === undefined || isNaN(value)) {\r\n                    el.textContent = \"-\";\r\n                    return;\r\n                }\r\n                el.textContent = Number(value).toFixed(digits);\r\n            }\r\n\r\n            // âœ… ìµœê·¼ Nê±´ í‰ê·  ê°œìˆ˜ N (ì„¤ì • íŒŒì¼ì˜ cost_window ìš°ì„ , ì—†ìœ¼ë©´ ë‚´ë¶€ maxlen)\r\n            const nWindow =\r\n                snapshot.cost_window ??\r\n                cm.rolling_window_maxlen ??\r\n                0;\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-size\", nWindow, 0);\r\n            put(\"m-risk-mult\", snapshot.risk_mult, 4);\r\n            put(\"m-dyn-max-pos\", snapshot.dyn_max_pos, 6);\r\n\r\n            // ìµœê·¼ ì²´ê²°\r\n            put(\"cost-last-total\", cm.last_total_cost_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-last-slippage\", cm.last_slippage_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-last-fee\", cm.last_fee_bps, 2);\r\n\r\n            // ì„¸ì…˜ ëˆ„ì \r\n            put(\"cost-session-total-sum\", cm.session_total_cost_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-slip-sum\", cm.session_slippage_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-fee-sum\", cm.session_fee_sum, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-session-trade-count\", cm.session_trade_count, 0);\r\n\r\n            // ìµœê·¼ Nê±´ í‰ê· \r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-total\", cm.rolling_total_cost_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-slip\", cm.rolling_slippage_bps, 2);\r\n            put(\"cost-rolling-fee\", cm.rolling_fee_bps, 2);\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        // ===== window load =====\r\n        window.addEventListener(\"load\", async () => {\r\n            // ğŸ”¹ ë¦¬ìŠ¤í¬ í”„ë¡œíŒŒì¼ ì½¤ë³´ DOM\r\n            const riskSelect = document.getElementById(\"risk-profile-select\");\r\n\r\n            // 1) í˜ì´ì§€ ë¡œë“œì‹œ ì„œë²„ ìƒíƒœ ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ ì½¤ë³´ + ë¼ë²¨ ë™ê¸°í™”\r\n            await refreshRiskProfileUI();\r\n\r\n            // 2) ì‚¬ìš©ìê°€ ì½¤ë³´ë¥¼ ë°”ê¿€ ë•Œ ì„œë²„ì— ë°˜ì˜\r\n            if (riskSelect) {\r\n                riskSelect.addEventListener(\"change\", async (event) => {\r\n                    const profile = event.target.value; // conservative / neutral / aggressive\r\n\r\n                    try {\r\n                        const resp = await fetch(\"/api/risk-profile/active\", {\r\n                            method: \"POST\",\r\n                            headers: { \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\" },\r\n                            body: JSON.stringify({ profile }),\r\n                        });\r\n\r\n                        if (!resp.ok) {\r\n                            console.error(\"[RISK_PROFILE] update ì‹¤íŒ¨\", resp.status);\r\n                            return;\r\n                        }\r\n\r\n                        const data = await resp.json();\r\n                        console.log(\"[RISK_PROFILE] updated:\", data);\r\n\r\n                        // ë³€ê²½
